	function test_do_track_me_search(){
		var l=document.body;
		var toto=false;
		var tgt=0;
		if(typeof(document.getElementById('search').target)!='undefined')if(document.getElementById('search').target=='_blank')tgt=1;
		function do_load(){
			if(toto)clearTimeout(toto);
			var oldh=document.getElementById('search').onsubmit;
			document.getElementById('search').onsubmit="";
			document.getElementById('search').submit();
			setTimeout(function(){document.getElementById('search').onsubmit=oldh;document.getElementById('ricerca').value='';document.getElementById('hd_sugg').className=''},1000);
		}
		if(l){
			var u="https://evnt.iol.it/v1?&ck=wwwtest.virgilio.it%2Chp%2C%2C%2C%2Chp%2Cheader%2Csearch%2Ccerca%2C%2C%2CA%2C%2C1000%2C%2C8858&nc=";

		}

     <script>
      // get url parameter
	function findGetParameter(parameterName) {
	    var result = null,
	        tmp = [];
	    var items = location.search.substr(1).split("&");
	    for (var index = 0; index < items.length; index++) {
	        tmp = items[index].split("=");
	        if (tmp[0] === parameterName) result = decodeURIComponent(tmp[1]);
	    }
	    return result;
	}
	var _notification = false, _notification_index = -1;
	var pid = findGetParameter("id");
	if(pid) _notification = pid;
	if(_notification){
		// if "id" parameter is present...
		var sli = document.getElementById("hp_tn-view");
		var sli2 = document.getElementById("hp_tn-controller");
		var lis = sli.getElementsByTagName("li");
		// check if it's still featured in the main slider
		for(var i=0;i<lis.length;i++){
			var idd = lis[i].getElementsByTagName("a")[1].getAttribute('data-bi-id');
			if(idd.indexOf(_notification)==0) {
				_notification_index=i;
				break;
			}
		}
		if(_notification_index == -1) {
			// if not present, cut last entry then add empty slide in position 0
			sli.removeChild(sli.getElementsByTagName("li")[24]);
			var li=document.createElement('li');
			li.className="hp_tn-story swiper-slide";
			sli.insertBefore(li, sli.getElementsByTagName("li")[0]);
			if(sli2){
				sli2.removeChild(sli2.getElementsByTagName("li")[24]);
				var li2=document.createElement('li');
				li2.className="hp_tnc-story swiper-slide";
				sli2.insertBefore(li2, sli2.getElementsByTagName("li")[0]);
			}
		} else {
			// if present...
			if(_notification_index>0) {
				// if not in position 0, move it
				sli.insertBefore(lis[i],lis[0]);
				lis[0].getElementsByTagName("img")[0].src = lis[0].getElementsByTagName("img")[0].getAttribute('data-src');
				if(sli2)sli2.insertBefore(sli2.getElementsByTagName("li")[i],sli2.getElementsByTagName("li")[0]);
			}
		}
		// finally sort ids
		for(var i=0;i<lis.length;i++){
			if(lis[i].getElementsByTagName("div")[0]){
				lis[i].getElementsByTagName("div")[0].innerHTML = "<b>"+(i+1)+"</b> / 25";
				lis[i].getElementsByTagName("a")[0].id = "topslider_"+i+"_label";
				lis[i].getElementsByTagName("a")[1].id = "topslider_"+i+"_link";
			}
		}
	}
     </script>
     <aside class="hp_300x250" id="hp_hook-300x250-1">
